0.0 (22):
CREATE VIEW "webauthn2_db"."attributesummary" AS
  WITH RECURSIVE taa(aid, taid) AS (
      SELECT aid, aid FROM "webauthn2_db"."attribute"
    UNION
      SELECT base.aid, recur.parent
      FROM taa AS base
      JOIN "webauthn2_db"."nestedattribute" AS recur ON (base.taid = recur.child)
  ),

  tua2 AS (
    SELECT ua.id AS username, array_agg(DISTINCT a.attribute) AS attributes
    FROM "webauthn2_db"."userattribute" AS ua
    JOIN taa ON (ua.aid = taa.aid)
    JOIN "webauthn2_db"."attribute" AS a ON (taa.taid = a.aid)
    GROUP BY ua.id
  ),

  taa2 AS (
    SELECT taa.aid AS aid, array_agg(a.attribute) AS attributes
    FROM taa
    JOIN "webauthn2_db"."attribute" AS a ON (taa.taid = a.aid)
    GROUP BY taa.aid
  ),

  aa2 AS (
    SELECT aa.child AS aid, array_agg(DISTINCT a.attribute) AS attributes
    FROM (SELECT * FROM "webauthn2_db"."nestedattribute" UNION SELECT aid, aid FROM "webauthn2_db"."attribute") AS aa
    JOIN "webauthn2_db"."attribute" AS a ON (aa.parent = a.aid)
    GROUP BY aa.child
  ),

  ua2 AS (
    SELECT ua.id, array_agg(DISTINCT a.attribute) AS attributes
    FROM "webauthn2_db"."userattribute" AS ua
    JOIN "webauthn2_db"."attribute" AS a ON (ua.aid = a.aid)
    GROUP BY ua.id
  )

  SELECT
    ua2.id AS name,
    'client' AS type,
    ua2.attributes AS direct_attributes,
    tua2.attributes AS all_attributes
  FROM ua2
  LEFT OUTER JOIN tua2 ON (ua2.id = tua2.username)

UNION

  SELECT
    a.attribute AS name,
    'attribute' AS type,
    aa2.attributes AS direct_attributes,
    taa2.attributes AS all_attributes
  FROM "webauthn2_db"."attribute" a
  LEFT OUTER JOIN aa2 ON (a.aid = aa2.aid)
  LEFT OUTER JOIN taa2 ON (a.aid = taa2.aid)

;
